# 2-6 数据库加密设计

大家好，我是大木。这节课来探讨数据库加密设计。我们主要还是围绕 MySQL 去探讨。项目中有一些敏感的信息，有加密的需求，保护数据免受黑客获取是一个非常重要的问题。这部分来说，有三种解决方案，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/c9530b59-fd11-4675-b5c9-5cfc1e9244a5/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=ad719289cfcc2c4c73bf08c006c17d018f8ad0bd456edbd03c0fa0870c8f7f18&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

一是在数据库层面处理，二是在应用层面处理，三是在传输层处理。先来看第一种，在数据库层面处理。 MySQL 提供了一系列加解密的函数，例如 encode decode、DS、encrypt、 DS decrypt 等等。我很遗憾，这些函数从 MySQL 5. 7 开始已经废弃，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/a2972e10-8c7a-455b-8413-4b617090d57b/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=eb8eb29d975d9cda44457d2a2bded133db2eeda398a1ab01ae5714dcb471f999&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

到 MySQL 8. 0 已经被删除了。在这里，在这篇文档，这是一篇 MySQL 5. 7 的文档，里面有说这些函数已经被deprecated，也就是废弃了。而在这篇文档，这是一篇 MySQL 8. 0 的文档，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/c84e28c7-a532-40b2-9abc-0aeb7d65fed9/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=46ae8e4c183fdaeab143ca2b7cd2a66c46e6b27dc708ada3dc99c7bd34263a4e&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

里面有说这些函数已经被删除了，回到 p p t ， 应该怎么办？

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/f1ed2cc3-1dd9-4bf8-b30f-978f0feb13ec/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=95987d91e62132f0867c8f729475b6385cdc23a262ea5728cf83ec40729dba72&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

现在 MySQL 的加密函数只剩下了  aes_encrypt 以及 aes_decrypt。从函数名称就可以看出来，它是基于 aes 算法实现的。


加解密来看一下怎么玩儿。用 aes_encrypt 传入明文以及密钥就可以加密。用 aes_decrypt 传入密文以及密钥就可以解密。这个里的密钥要和前面加密的密钥保持一致，还是比较简单的。但这个函数有几个注意点，不妨通过实验来说明。在这里我准备了一张表，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/95daa22b-b54d-48fe-b24b-3aec7a41b6e0/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=8dc2c7ef23ac65e0d0baf8900ce539233fe88fcc4eb5d09c46d8bdb3a79c5a84&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

叫做test。


a e s，里面有这么几个字段，其中有 binary , Blob 这几个基于二进制的字段，以及两个 varchar 字段。 column_varchar_utf-8 是基于 UTF 8 字符集的，而 column varchar latin 则是基于 Latin 1 字符集的。我们先来把表创建一下。使用 show full columns from test 看一下字段的详情。

而 column_varchar_Latin 则是基于 latin1_ swedish_ci 这样的字符集。表创建完成之后，是一条 insert 的语句,这里用 aes_encrypt 包裹了每一个字段，

实现所有字段的加密存储。同时传入的密钥都是key_pass。实际项目里面，我们可以为不同的字段设置不同的密钥。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/fe4f93b7-a7e9-4ed8-833d-942218a595e9/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=a56d7f2783a695025e2deb1ca1912304c8a74d193c6c3c392aa88ec39fe38c78&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)


自己看一看，可以看到执行报错，他说 column _varchar_ utf8 这个字段没有办法存储这一段东西，这其实就是加密后的内容。于是我们可以得到第一个结论。结论一此命令执行失败。 utf8 字符集的 varchar  字段无法存储加密后的数据。


再来看第二条 insert 的语句，和前面基本一样，只是把 column_varchar_ utf8 给去掉了。执行看一看，可以看到执行成功。进到数据库里面，可以看到数据存储也是 OK 的。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/12d7724a-e451-4627-a468-0a782a300103/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=d2b1d2b53f5a5f068ad93941d0256efff08e02b83b8dbd0d9a179ff374bd5fe9&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

于是我们可以得到第二个结论执行成功。 Latin1 字符集的 varchar 字段可以存储加密后的数据。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/e9042a70-4cfe-44c1-b1cc-17c75143cebe/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=849bda27a438adece8a6d88ebd919aa5ed2a2659219b9ec0951f274a412b0924&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

除此以外，我们还发现 binary 以及 Blob 也可以存储加密后的数据。


Blob 可以存储加密后的数据，为什么varbinary 以及 blob 底层都是基于二进制存储的,存储后的加密数据我们怎么获取呢？

只要用 aes_decrypt 传入字段以及加密时候的密钥就可以解密了,执行可以看到能够正常获取明文

讲到这里，大家不禁要想，实际项目里面我们可能不可避免的需要用字符串存储加密后的数据，而同时我们可能并不想设置这样的字符集。怎么让

基于 utf8 的 varchar 类型的字段存储加密后的数据？


有两种方案。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/ecf817f5-b692-458a-a862-7683c35e8aa5/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=97bf35f01f7ff648774208076b4fba16095276b978b082e32566cf48f14e459f&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

第一种方案把加密后的数据用 hex 包裹一下，转成十六进制再去存储。执行看看，可以看到执行成功，解密的话只要用 unhex 把加密后的内容转成二进制，

再用 aes decrypt 进行解密就可以了。执行，可以看到能够正常解密，记录一下。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/9217b36d-2d02-4333-a775-b70af3564724/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=290be0650327ac1cae32b817984dd7f2f0aa2cc7bdb4640b2c282f18324f7051&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

解决方案一，用 hex 转十六进制存储。


除此以外，还有解决方案 2 用 to_base64 把加密后的内容转 base 64存储。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/652395a0-bcb1-4416-991c-aa172a819252/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=fb10af10c9092e83bd57b4d954a59833b29593e6dacbac40d337e373932a1595&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

inserts 可以看到也能插入成功。在查询的时候，可以把加密后的内容用 from_base64 转成二进制再去解密，也可以正常解密，记录一下。


解决方案 2 转 base 64 删除。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/c7110ef6-e85b-4727-ae84-2fe0c8a04b3e/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=3f41dc20a6af746fdf7b4d2fb5ae1a174e61eebfcf66133cb249d6a1235aa2fd&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

同时我们还发现第二行数据，也就是之前 hex 存储的数据。因为用这条 SQL 没有办法解密，所以直接返回了空记录下。对于无法解密的数据， aes_decrypt 会直接返回 none。这是有关 aes encrypt 以及 as decrypt 的几个结论。


下面我们来看一下如果用 spring data jpa 以及 mybatis，该怎么样和 aes_encrypt 以及 aes_decrypt 的配合。

这是一个基于 spring data JPA 的例子。首先做了一个存储，之后又做了一个查询，来看下实体的定义。实地里面我们使用了 @ColumnTransformer 这样的注解，

并且使用了 read 属性,以及 write 属性的属性做读取， read 属性做写入，也就是增删改。在这里插入的时候，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/ba26af22-87a1-4327-b668-dd6a23344dd2/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=1013a9e12388aecef314619b039b666f091430ce8b1c1cb791e2c3ea3ee8c052&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

Hibernate 会自动用这里的 AES_ENCRIPT 问号填入这里的值，并传入这里的key，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/b08ac272-91f7-4171-9bb5-ecca3563964e/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=6883db87a939ad1342cc020436f0b8197bb22aa6b6737b1678d4b1fc05b7f151&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

自动加密。而在做读取的时候， 

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/f1b0ee6c-0915-49c0-ba23-02ec799208fa/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466SZMCD77U%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICLRSznXR6MFY8ebJAYy1wzadzYmERujBtOM3XBU7WZOAiEA%2FyvTokfj6YDm5wbMHF1OK%2F4tmxhty2P7G0Har6BeMakqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDFU3NvU7MUUk2dPnfyrcAxxU7mzPxFpGnsrkHO8di%2BWTdC242I1cKNzPFpJ4pFzi4i806F1cqKIHtvl5cgM%2FTQn4wqySEWBk%2Fb8JnfhmRcKXla9kBIlVOQ63ENncEnDhrcn4EQ%2BUjM3v3MMZNCqElvZbqRkrS8gWxUX88sFxatGGcWCrujdKvGQSi93f0auSIlxzKeXiCVFJsnxxcdGQISJP9QHo4rkadKsSiscdlMLiZjKXTbXL9UWgxvh1i6mZs%2B4coJrPKRvOMO0UGybTaKeUNpLO2JPTooh9RccqeSuBI%2FJXrHfz0lPHI7JI7K0dk5RswXNwPssmeJcNQMkjhJco5ePQ3Pn95YJ8Gfw2qO0UsVo3NXUNxT5q3onOTI195DvRoYQq8aYulTZIucxGq9Pte3158deCrcR5I%2FSKfU2gpnkUUhYXFmcPb7iS4swquItX6fLhTztBPgx5FoxKmzUYNz%2FodauWnFMoB%2F1pAnClC30MJFYpb%2FlNhXv2FhJEM08k6vrqIBuGRE7Q%2FPE03W6Xe5YN63oABA6SzJxjZp%2FmMEC0wYu3tQElcaY7VYRNKtUcPy6AJu0mJej44vWuOqdC5waLyKremMXkjNu1Ub8UcAHNg4iXaWF%2BSFdWxWwPbqu9ndieC43F7dVLMNa6%2F9IGOqUB3gIrtmaY3nRY4dRlwYR9N4YwYDGwDFNgrAy74XucuzdYXlayslibEzmKqUbTMz7nVKPLF7ZV1OtforEq%2FwWKY1nqiUp9teKhj0lxpISX3KwzmMRuRRkgFlJocVIQ%2BkBVfTeqNZ99nIU0GjvZRTV4jWRukUH6%2B1JaxoW7g9rMua6BtolOHfGU4gebA7X9APAhseeoZlBcjznm82p9vkpkLUz3gfiV&X-Amz-Signature=28fa76a2fc16ce1dc17dc3cf555f0aee359f3d305554ab0c6503f6619492e710&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

Hibernate 会自动把读到的结果用这么一段进行处理，也就是用 AES_DECRPT 的进行解密，并用 CAST 把它转成了一个 char 。


对于 utf8 字符级的字符串来说也是类似的。在插入的时候可以套一个HEX，

的时候可以用 UNHEX 启动。


下了。边前看看那个 host 8088 j p a，可以看到能够正常返回铭文。

我们在插入的时候都使用 AES_ENCRIPT 或者是在外面套 HEX 的方式进行插入。而查询的时候，我们需要在传入的明文条件上面加密，

加密完全是由代码去实现的。而查询的时候，我们的 selected 去 sql

 上面也不会做任何的处理。


内容的解密也是由 AESUtil.decrypt 去实现的。

这种方式大家应该是非常熟悉的，比方存储密码这样的字段往往采用的都是这种方式对吧。

并且 AesUtil 已经实现了 MySQL 的 AESUtil.encrypt 以及 AES_DECRPYT 的功能。


你的加密和解密的效果和之前 MySQL 函数的用法是一样的，甚至可以互相通用。比方用函数加密，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/7d886d53-14c4-40ee-ace3-40ba26c2d7d5/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=4f562222cdfe497ffaa8b9ddd10d3b779176c235cb454ec1581124c53b949960&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

用 decrypt 的方法解密。唯一的区别在于这个工具类，它在加密以及解密的时候，要求密钥的长度要是 16 尾，否则就会报错。如果你的密钥不够 16 位，可以在末尾补零，这样得到了效果，才可以和 MySQL 的这两个函数得到了结果一致。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/fa0e36de-58a5-478e-b822-a7e2f59c773c/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=860d35e5f4b2a21adcfad997cc57ac2697f76f42ac49ea0f91688be6818e46d6&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

当然了，实际项目里面你也不一定要用 AES 算法，你完全可以使用其他的算法。这是第二种方式。


第三种方式在传输层处理。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/e3670d2e-585c-491d-8023-31354ace2b16/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=3422bad04529e6eb800af4353be23ecb2b93450085d26be4d10b2086aacc1f9b&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

它是支持 SSL的。而 SSL 具备数据加密、身份验证、消息完整性验证等等机制，这样可以防止传输过程中数据被窃取等等问题。 MySQL 怎么样使用SSL？这里面的细节还是挺多的，所以我专门写了一篇文章，一起来看一下。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/a9f570b6-78b0-4c6c-ab6f-917b41b7b286/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=7a59bef9889bbaf867ae492f80d1ccfc77f213cd3663b861113464520a817fc1&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

有关 ssl 首先从 MySQL 的 5. 7 开始默认支持的。你可以用 show variables like ‘have_ssl’； 去查看当前 MySQL 是不是已经支持了SSL。执行一下。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/a3e79b50-2e8c-4596-baac-ac09a9eaf5db/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=49e265c1f903d47526a6efe9bacddf8615b98d6f6a5e667e976e85b9a0c05bc9&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

由于我 MySQL 版本是八点零点二二，所以默认支持的。如果你使用的 MySQL 版本比较老，可以参考这里的文章去配置一下，从而开启SSL。我们可以用 idea 去连接数据库看看。


点击，点击 test connection 可以看到这里 SSL 是yes，说明现在连接 MySQL 的时候已经使用了SSL。下面来看一下 SSL 相关的几个参数，主要有这么 3 个。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/6aba78e7-9954-4456-b434-2fe0a15f80f4/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=f72ea9392d47fea0aadd849b694a681a12be3b6502ea0fdf48d1493c118d776d&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/b1b687ab-ce61-46b6-b56b-4a68a3585650/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=f8a3eca951fa1ea9cee774e713bf1b7e5d740c1228bd333d612e75c26c16f6b6&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

首先 useSSL 表示是否开启SSL，是否要使用 ssrL去连接MySQL，默认情况下就是true，因此我们刚刚什么都没有，配 SSL 就是yes。


第二个参数是 verifyServerCertificate。这个配置是当 useSSL 等于 true，用来控制 MySQL 驱动是不是要校验服务器端的证书。此外还有一个 requireSSL，是当 useSSR 配置人数，是不是强制要求 server 端要支持SSL？也就是可能有这种场景。虽然我们连接数据库的时候配置了 useSSL 等于 true，但是数据库它并不支持 SSL。这个东西可以用来做一个校验。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/3fb65c80-bab4-4940-a2d8-154596a86838/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=088bb6cfcffc4f665322fb4706ceff725022389e5970f0e8207a3f755c64845c&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

从 MySQL connector 8.0.13开始，又额外引入了 sslMode 参数，这个参数可以用来简化 SSL 的配置， sslMode 就相当于是这 3 个配置的组合。这里我写了 SSL Mode 的几种取值，以及它相当于这种方式的哪几个配置的组合。 sslMode 这种参数比较的新，考虑到国内 MySQL 驱动的使用情况，我们课上还是使用这种方式

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/2075b968-752b-4b6e-9f52-a9037eafdffe/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=5c4e01842febecdf252947cb8fb3fd7daad7351c62762989c377b69e4ebaa1eb&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

去配置。


除此以外，你还可以在服务器端配置这样的参数，

强制要求客户端用 SSL 连接数据库。默认情况下，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/a0d8c806-965d-489a-b8cf-bafb2754144e/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=36ab7a1fa4128952fe99e56888829a6c4be6a3345f87e9b85b0ac978cf18866f&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

这个配置是 off，也就是服务器端，它并不会强制客户端用 SSL 连接自己。除此以外，有个 ssl 还有几种认证方式服务器端认证、客户端认证以及双向认证。

大家看这里我们没有在 URL 上面添加任何参数，

也就是现在使用的是 useSSL等于true。verifyServerCertificate=false requireSSL也是false。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/562026e1-dca5-4342-8d55-6878506340ca/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=a35104ff3bdb09b26a6f053b7ef696291fc8135d0b940ceca158aa3d2eeb7ce7&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

在这种情况下，我们的 MySQL 驱动会无条件的信任 server 单的证书。如果我们希望比较好的安全性，应该把 verify server certificate 设成 true 对吧？

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/72c08bf2-e003-4ae1-abfb-a8a8d9ef8bb7/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=f063f072f583ccb4d4d95bc380169804a900fa5fbe1c61afbd6aef32fa11af8e&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

这样可以校验服务器端的证书。而由于服务器端的证书，它是一个自签名的证书，所以一旦把这两个参数设成true，就会报错。来试一下， and test，可以看到报错了。

怎么样解决这种问题？ MySQL 提供了三种认证方式 client 端认证以及双向认证。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/829d3eb8-c782-45a2-bbba-ffb2603d9bde/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=98fcf9b373d2c43e43fefca8c6bb8cb626a37cdae8ef1d8d27105f88e1f2f2ed&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

玩法大概是这样的首先去拷贝，这 3 个文件都在 MySQL 的数据存储目录，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/33caa3de-e023-4de1-ad76-b09644a50843/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=289ad79a639f4a4cfd8c4bf70023de4f841c72aa7cae52eb2dc0ba77f63d1ef7&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

默认情况下都在这里。如果你找不到在哪里，可以使用命令去查看数据目录在哪里，事情可以看到，在这里。我已经拷贝好了。在这里。最后我们来试一下单向认证 server 端。首先需要生成 trust store，你可以把这里的 allies 以及 surpass 改成你想要的值copy。

打开终端，执行

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/32afc732-bf93-4e8a-a7b6-ebd92604e645/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231155Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=268cbcb1c39a702e8f00662711372e3cd0fbce31489f298adaf008a38c10f786&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

。猪肉是添加成功。这样就会在当前目录生成一个名为 trust store 的文件。之后可以用这三种方式的任意一种去连接数据库。

首先需要把 client key 给转换成 P12 这种格式

。这里的 name pass out 里面的密码以及文件你都可以自己去指定。 copy 粘贴完成。

并且现在我们的连接方式其实是双向认证的。


有同学可能要说了，在 application.yml 里面我们应该怎么配，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/0ada643b-f741-4ea2-b76e-fb32f4fb9c23/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=fa118ff061858ef672064875aa873491c3e122def81dc6308cc2726ad6e249f5&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

可以这样玩。这里我使用大于号可以实现多行配置，它会把这么一大段里面的空格全部给截掉，这样的阅读起来就比较的清晰。一些。启动项目看一看，可以发现依然能够成功启动，刷新也能够正常返回，结果没有问题。


这是在传输层处理。简单总结一下，这节课我们探讨了 MySQL 数据加密的 3 种方式。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/8f8f8aa5-d5bb-4f2d-aa39-888a4402a334/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=0169e73b76428d1691b302720ed6cdf528f905c6b9ae87dda7f8247ec47f78b7&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

一是在数据层面处理，我们着重探讨了 as encrypt 以及 as decrypt，并且总结了几个结论。同时还讲解了 spring data g、p、 a 以及 Mybeddis 怎么样和这两个函数配合使用。第二种方式在应用层面处理，也就是用代码去实现加解密。第三种方式在传输层面处理，我们着重探讨了 MySQL 怎么样使用 SSL 实现加密传输，同时探讨了 SSL 相关的一些参数和注意点。


最后来总结一下 3 种方式的特点。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/904801f2-6ff4-4500-a371-ad022e52fbdb/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4662WPARSRH%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231156Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIBUA88LMdl0PUGH8MGOfgr%2BHjouWYcQyOJy0h7wQD2ZAAiAJ5dVbG8G1T6QKLtvs2%2FQVAk6K8opJJziBok%2BDlflGRSqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIM4LBF5MiDgCcb9tnzKtwDouzjzLLbbYiDahjukVDqQiNoT0xhPvBUrAOcR%2FTGqjGB2J5%2F%2FeGD6rvZKKXuj13vQdWbtLr9lEtgeCMq4TTa065Tnwzp0FvVsYhm9ZASKabqli24KDZThZCzEAsK%2BmVYNT8w6P0GG%2Bp2XHZPq1ubK0ux%2FynZiuopf4PO4ofX%2F7zXoMIw8FOVFd9fdZEbyj4voZBnWtm8MlJtcUfj0xOzBPYLFk1dg0JB0l3ZX%2BqEJc%2BmdQzqA5P4ZQp8HUT%2BHuv3%2FNuFUQ5NRXq%2FYtirYOVmGjQgJ3CTf63c%2FLML9E%2BFzNDT6UHifAlH7j24zFUh9k7%2B2da%2FLjQX%2B%2FOzMEegM%2F9jrUBqDq6epUirrc3%2FCV8hs8WjFx5Qaqr1sz1eJjGMYz4Wo81kYQy6R5tUNpshhOaB6c3PSMOJAoQOUOm%2FtiDcMqVvh6wEDS3jyThN85R4xgTHKhbRCYTsGmax2GlZ7UK35qwYZj7RT1r4i3jAw9bQ6ZxdUZp7pVvACTAVeZbJIdq0ku9nvng3%2BYlmZj33lm29xhP7NB%2B9qaQ%2Bk%2BnzCTSEXdhOVfNasx%2FNzZ4lWfywn2vKK2vVU0Mt8KOsnhEYNfeIbrnmi7YuYOk5xq3Z7gXjY6Y0xlJBAZynQhMPsRww17r%2F0gY6pgEZVHKTgqwnE1Gyw%2F0tIX6xqN1N%2BCOh7A0kJfsWGpu6vIAE2xCyw%2B0R76vZ38grjBb1fBINBq8XfWwvHe3LKW%2BXBFOOdSFlXiEDrwPdaimwYZUuF2GvS7KLzIdiQM4uN6OykjNe4JEt0YJNi6vu%2Bp0F7xO8pLFy0btGFvcCLqaVc7CHGtoFqbGAiO%2BCnTRPQzFwbJJqZ9lautmrh%2B5XtfMe8uI60Nkd&X-Amz-Signature=00e3a2682e717560ef1d0d4007698bd065bc552c7f4897d1039dcadb7a2af52a&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

在数据库层面处理，它的特点是实现比较简单，函数包一下就 OK 了，但是注意点有点多。另外，支持的算法比较有限，目前只支持a、s，如果想用其他的算法就无能为力了。在应用层面处理是最灵活的代码想怎么写，而在传输层面处理实现应该说是最简单的。默认情况下支持 SSL 传输的，并且比较省心，维护成本也是非常低的，可以基本上没有成本，即使你需要去配置证书，也只要配置一次就 OK 了。在实际项目里面，建议大家优先使用s、 l 的方式。如果你的数据非常的敏感，你不仅担心传输层面的问题，可以在数据库层面处理，或者在应用层面处理。我个人更加倾向于在应用层面处理的方式，因为这种方式比数据库层面灵活很多。这节课就到这里，谢谢大家。
